 Hollywood stars George Clooney and Antonio Banderas are famous worldwide for their fetish eyes (bedroom eye), but a new study has shown that in the eyes of women, such men with nayan maps are sly rather than romantic
 daily mail ke anusaar michigan vishvavidhyalay ke shodhakartaaon ke ek dal ke adhyayan se pataa chalaa he ki iske vipareet jo mard mahilaon par saamaanya tareeke se or khuli ankhon se nihaarte hai unhen zyada eemaandaar or acha sahyogi mana jaataa he
 This research has been published in livescience
 is shodh main 400 stri or purushon ne hissaa liya
 According to the report, the researchers showed two groups of half-open eyes and fully open-eyed photographs of 20- to 22-year-old men
 unase poocha gaya ki ve kitne aakarshith hai or kya ve unke saath dirghagami rishta chahengi

 ) Sheikh Hasina was sworn in as the Prime Minister of Bangladesh on Monday for the third consecutive term
 iske saath hi shaikh hasina record chauthi baar bangladesh kii pradhanmantri ban gayi
 His party Awami League won a landslide victory in the December 30 elections
 raashtrapati mohammad abdul hamid ne bangabhavan main 71 varshiya hasina ko pad kii shapath dilaai
 This is Hasina's fourth term as Prime Minister
 raashtrapati ne uske baad sarkaar main shaamil hone vaale nae mantriyon, rajya mantriyon or up mantriyon ko pad kii shapath dilaai
 Hasina's cabinet will have 24 ministers, 22 ministers of state
